### Round 3: Bahrain Grand Prix
*Date: 2004-04-04*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 14: Belgian Grand Prix
*Date: 2004-08-29*

#### Qualifying Results

### Round 18: Brazilian Grand Prix
